\[ \begin{equation*} \log M(f) = \frac {1}{2\pi }\int _0^{2\pi } \log \left\lvert f(e^{it})\right\rvert dt. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} f(z)=a_{m}\prod _{k=1}^{m}{(z-\alpha _k)}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} M(f) = |a_m|\prod _{k=1}^{m-1} \max \{1,|\alpha _k|\} \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} M(f) = \lim _{p\to 0^+} \left\lVert f\right\rVert _p, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left\lVert f\right\rVert _p = \left(\frac {1}{2\pi }\int _0^{2\pi } \left\lvert f(e^{it})\right\rvert ^p dt\right)^{1/p}, \qquad p > 0. \end{equation*} \]

\[ c_1\sqrt {n} \leq |f_n(z)| \leq c_2\sqrt {n}, \qquad z \in {\mathbb{C}}, \quad |z|=1. \]

\[ (1-\varepsilon )\sqrt {n} \leq |f_n(z)| \leq (1+\varepsilon ) \sqrt {n}, \qquad z \in {\mathbb{C}}, \quad |z|=1, \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \sup _{f\in \mathfrak{U}_n} \frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}} = 1 \tag{1.1}\cssId{eqnFielding1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \underset {f\in \mathfrak{U}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}} \geq e^{-\gamma /2}\left(1+O\left(n^{-1/4+\varepsilon }\right)\right), \tag{1.2}\cssId{eqnFielding2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \underset {f \in \mathfrak{U}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \left( F(f) \right) := \frac {1}{(2\pi )^n}\int _0^{2\pi }\int _0^{2\pi } \cdots \int _{0}^{2\pi } F(f) \,d\theta _0 \, d\theta _1 \,\cdots \, d\theta _{n-1}, \]

\[ f(z)=\sum _{j=0}^{n-1}{e^{i\theta _j}z^j}\,. \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{U}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left(\frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}}\right) = -\gamma /2 \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{U}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left(\frac {\left\lVert f\right\rVert _p}{\sqrt {n}}\right) = \frac {1}{p}\log \Gamma (1+p/2), \qquad p > 0. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{U}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}} = e^{-\gamma /2} \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{U}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {\left\lVert f\right\rVert _p^p}{\sqrt {n}} = \Gamma (1+p/2), \qquad p > 0. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \exp \left( \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left(\frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}}\right)\right) = e^{-\gamma /2} \tag{1.3}\cssId{texmlid2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}} = e^{-\gamma /2}, \tag{1.4}\cssId{texmlid3}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \exp \left( \underset {f\in \mathfrak{L}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {\| {\hat{f}}\|_p}{\sqrt {n}}\right) \right)=\Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p}, \qquad p > 0, \tag{1.5}\cssId{texmlid4}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{L}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {\left\lVert f\right\rVert _p}{\sqrt {n}} = \Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p}, \qquad p > 0. \tag{1.6}\cssId{texmlid1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} e^{-\gamma /2} \ge \limsup _{n\to \infty } \exp \left( \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}}\log \left( \frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}}\right) \right). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \liminf _{n\to \infty } \exp \left( \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}}\log \left( \frac {M(f)}{n^{1/2-\varepsilon }}\right) \right) \ge e^{-\gamma /2}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \frac {M(f_p)}{\left\lVert f_p\right\rVert _2} > \frac {1}{2}-\varepsilon \tag{1.7}\cssId{eqnEL}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {M(f)}{\left\lVert f\right\rVert _2} > e^{-\gamma /2} - \varepsilon , \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {M(f)}{\left\lVert f\right\rVert _2} < e^{-\gamma /2} + \varepsilon . \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \frac {1}{2^n}\left| \left\{ f \in \mathfrak{L}_n : \left| \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} - e^{-\gamma /2} \right| > \varepsilon \right\} \right| =0 \tag{1.8}\cssId{texmlid6}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \frac {1}{2^n}\left|\left\{ f \in \mathfrak{L}_n : \left| \frac {\| f\|_p}{\sqrt {n}} - \Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p} \right| > \varepsilon \right\} \right| =0 \tag{1.9}\cssId{texmlid5}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{L}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \left(\frac {\left\lVert f\right\rVert _p}{\sqrt {n}}\right)^\alpha =\left( \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{L}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {\left\lVert f\right\rVert _p}{\sqrt {n}}\right)^\alpha \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{L}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \left(\frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}}\right)^\alpha =\left( \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in \mathfrak{L}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}}\right)^\alpha \end{equation*} \]

\[ f(z):=\sum _{j=0}^{n-1}{a_jz^j}, \qquad z:=e^{i\theta }, \quad \theta \in [0,2\pi ), \]

\[ \begin{equation*} U_n:=U_n(f, \theta ) := \frac {|f(z)|^2}{n} = \frac {1}{n} \left| \sum _{j=0}^{n-1}a_je^{ij\theta } \right|^2. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \sigma _{n,c}^2 (\theta ) :=\sum _{j=0}^{n-1} \cos ^2(j\theta ) \;\; \mbox{ and } \;\; \sigma _{n,s}^2 (\theta ) :=\sum _{j=0}^{n-1} \sin ^2(j\theta ) \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} a_{k,n}(\theta ):=\frac {\cos (k\theta )}{\sigma _{n,c}(\theta )} \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} b_{k,n}(\theta ):=\frac {\sin (k\theta )}{\sigma _{n,s}(\theta )}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} C_n(\theta ):=\frac {\sum _{j=0}^{n-1}a_j\cos (j\theta )}{\sigma _{n,c}(\theta )} \;\; \mbox{ and } \;\; S_n(\theta ):=\frac {\sum _{j=0}^{n-1}a_j\sin (j\theta )}{\sigma _{n,s}(\theta )}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} U_n(f,\theta ) = \frac {|f(z)|^2}{n} = \frac {\sigma _{n,c}^2(\theta )C_n^2(\theta )+\sigma _{n,s}^2(\theta )S_n^2(\theta )}{n}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} F_n^z(x):= \frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \frac {|f(z)|^2}{n} \le x \right\} \right| \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} F_n^z(x) = F(x)+{{O}}(n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)}) \tag{2.10}\cssId{texmlid7}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ {\mathbb{E}}(|Z|^p) =\int _{-\infty }^{\infty } |x|^p d\Phi (x)=\frac {2^{p/2}\Gamma \left( (p+1)/2 \right)}{\sqrt {\pi }}, \]

\[ \Phi (x) =(1/\sqrt {2\pi })\int _{-\infty }^x {e^{-t^2/2} \,dt}. \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left| G_{n,c}(x)-\Phi (x)\right| \le c_3 \frac { \rho _n}{\sigma _n^3 \sqrt {n}} \quad \mbox{and } \quad \left| G_{n,s}(x)-\Phi (x)\right| \le c_3 \frac { \rho _n}{\sigma _n^3 \sqrt {n}}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \rho _n := {\mathbb{E}}(|X_n|^3), \qquad \lim _{n \rightarrow \infty } {\rho _n} = \frac {2^{3/2} \, \Gamma (2)}{\sqrt {\pi }} = 2\sqrt {\frac {2}{\pi }}, \]

\[ \sigma _n^2 := {\mathbb{E}}(|X_n|^2), \qquad \lim _{n \rightarrow \infty } {\sigma _n^2} = \frac {2 \, \Gamma (3/2)}{\sqrt {\pi }} = 1. \]

\[ \begin{equation*} G_{n,c}(x) = \Phi (x) + {{O}}(n^{-1/2})\;\; \mbox{ and }\;\; G_{n,s}(x) = \Phi (x) + {{O}}(n^{-1/2}) \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} \frac {\sigma _{n,c}^2}{n} & = & \frac {1}{n} \sum _{j=0}^{n-1}\cos ^2 (j\theta ) = \frac 12 + \frac {1}{2n} \sum _{j=0}^{n-1}\cos (2j\theta ) = \frac 12 + \frac {1}{2n}\Re \left( \sum _{j=0}^{n-1}e^{2ij\theta }\right) \\ & = & \frac 12 + {{O}}\left( \frac {1}{n\| 2 \theta \|} \right) = \frac 12 + {{O}}\left( n^{-(1-A)} \right) \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {\sigma _{n,c}^2}{n} = \frac 12 + {{O}}\left( n^{-(1-A)} \right) \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} & & \left| \frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \frac {(\sigma _{n,c}C_n)(\theta )}{\sqrt {n}} \leq x \right\}\right| - \Phi (x) \right| \\ & \le & \left| \frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \frac {(\sigma _{n,c}C_n)(\theta )}{\sqrt {n}} \leq x \right\}\right| - \frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : C_n(\theta ) \leq x \right\}\right| \right| \\ & & \qquad + \left|\frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : C_n(\theta ) \leq x\right\}\right| - \Phi (x) \right| \\ & \le & \left| \Phi \left( x\left(\frac 12+\frac {C}{n^{1-A}}\right)^{-1/2}\right) - \Phi \left( x\left(\frac 12-\frac {C}{n^{1-A}}\right)^{-1/2}\right) \right| + \left| G_{n,c}(x)-\Phi (x) \right| \\ & \ll & \frac {x}{n^{1-A}}e^{-c_4x^2} + n^{-1/2} \ll n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)} \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left| \frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \frac {(\sigma _{n,s}S_n)(\theta )}{\sqrt {n}} \leq x \right\}\right| - \Phi (x) \right| \ll n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {|f(z)|^2}{n}=\frac {\sigma _{n,c}^2(\theta )C_n(\theta )^2}{n} + \frac {\sigma _{n,s}^2(\theta )S_n(\theta )^2 }{n},\qquad z=e^{i\theta }. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} F_n^z(x)=F(x) + {{O}}(n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)}). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} G_n^z(t):=\frac {1}{2^n}\left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \le t\right\}\right|. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} G_n^z(t) & = & F_n^z(t). \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} G_n^z(t)= \begin{cases} F_n^z(t) & \mbox{ if $t \ge n^{-3},$} \\ 0 & \mbox{ if $t < n^{-3}.$} \end{cases} \tag{2.11}\cssId{a.0}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \left| \int _{0^+}^\infty \log t \; d \left( G_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| \le c_5 (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)}) \log n \tag{2.12}\cssId{texmlid8}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \left| \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \right) + \gamma \right| \le c_5 (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)}) \log n \tag{2.13}\cssId{texmlid12}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \right)= - \gamma , \tag{2.14}\cssId{texmlid24}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} & & \left| \int _n^\infty \log t \; d \left( G_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| \\ & = & \left| \int _n^\infty \log t \; d \left( F_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| \\ & = & \left| \left[ \left( F_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \log t \right]_n^\infty - \int _n^\infty \frac {F_n^z(t)-F(t)}{t}\; dt \right| \\ & \le & \left| \left[ \left( e^{-t} \right) \log t \right]_n^\infty \right| + \int _n^\infty {\frac {e^{-t}}{t}\; dt}, \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray} & & \left| \int _n^\infty \log t \; d \left( G_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| \le \frac {\log n}{e^n}+ \frac {1}{n} \int _n^\infty e^{-t} \; dt \ll \frac {\log n}{e^n}, \tag{2.15}\cssId{texmlid9}{}{} \end{eqnarray} \]

\[ \begin{align} & \left| \int _{1/n^3}^n \log t \; d \left( G_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| = \left| \int _{1/n^3}^n \log t \; d \left( F_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right|\tag{2.16}\cssId{texmlid10}{}{}\\ & = \left| \left[ \left( F_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \log t \right]_{1/n^3}^n - \int _{1/n^3}^n \frac {F_n^z(t)-F(t)}{t}\; dt \right| \\ & \ll \left| F_n^z(n)-F(n)\right| \log n + \left| F_n^z(n^{-3})-F(n^{-3})\right| \log n +\int _{1/n^3}^n \frac {|F_n^z(t)-F(t)|}{t}\; dt \\ & \ll (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)})\log n + (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)}) \int _{1/n^3}^n\frac {1}{t} \; dt \\ & \ll (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)})\log n. \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left| \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} \log t \; d \left( G_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| = \left| \left[ -F(t) \log t \right]_{0^+}^{1/n^3} + \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} \frac {F(t)}{t}\; dt \right| \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} & & \left| \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} \log t \; d \left(-F(t)\right) \right| \ll (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)})\log n + \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} {\frac {F(t)}{t}\; dt}. \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} \frac {F(t)}{t}\; dt = \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} \frac {1-e^{-t}}{t}\; dt \le \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} 1\; dt = \frac {1}{n^3} , \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \left| \int _{0^+}^{1/n^3} \log t \; d \left( G_n^z(t)-F(t)\right) \right| \ll (n^{-1/2}+n^{-(1-A)})\log n. \tag{2.17}\cssId{texmlid11}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \limsup _{n\to \infty } \frac {1}{2^n} \left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \min \left\{ \left| f(z) \right|: z\in {\mathbb{C}}\mbox{ and } ||z|-1|<\varepsilon n^{-2}\right\} < \varepsilon n^{-1/2}\right\}\right| \le c_6 \varepsilon \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} A_n(\varepsilon ) = \bigg \{ f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \min _{|z|=1}|f(z)| < \varepsilon n^{-1/2} \bigg \}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \limsup _{n\to \infty } \frac {1}{2^n}|A_n(\varepsilon )| \le c_6 \varepsilon \tag{2.18}\cssId{texmlid13}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ H_n := \{ \theta \in [0,2\pi ): \, \| 2\theta \| \ge n^{-1/2} \} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n \to \infty } {\frac {1}{2\pi } \int _{H_n} {\underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \right) \; d\theta }} = -\gamma . \end{equation*} \]

\[ -3 \log n = \log (n^{-3}) \leq \log (|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2/n) \leq \log n, \quad z = e^{i\theta }, \quad \theta \in [0,2\pi ). \]

\[ \begin{equation*} -3\log n \leq \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \right) \leq \log n, \quad \theta \in [0,2\pi ), \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {-6\log n}{\sqrt {n}} \leq \int _{[0,2\pi ) \setminus H_n}{\underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} {\, \log \left( \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \right) \, d\theta }} \leq \frac {2\log n}{\sqrt {n}}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n \to \infty } {\frac {1}{2\pi } \int _{[0,2\pi ) \setminus H_n} {\underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {|{\hat{f}}(z)|^2}{n} \right) \; d\theta }} = 0, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray} \underset {f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}}\frac {M(f)}{\sqrt {n}} & = & \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}}\frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}}+ \frac {1}{2^n} \sum _{f\in A_n(\varepsilon )} \frac {M(f)- M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}}. \tag{2.19}\cssId{b.1}{}{} \end{eqnarray} \]

\[ \begin{equation} 1 \leq M(f) \leq M({\hat{f}}) \leq \|{\hat{f}}\|_2 \leq \|f\|_2 + \|1/n\|_2 = n^{1/2} + n^{-1/2} \leq 2n^{1/2} \tag{2.20}\cssId{e.1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \limsup _{n\to \infty } \left| \frac {1}{2^n} \sum _{f\in A_n(\varepsilon )} \frac {M(f)- M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} \right| \le 2\limsup _{n\to \infty }\frac {1}{2^n}|A_n(\varepsilon )|\le 2c_6\varepsilon . \tag{2.21}\cssId{texmlid16}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \liminf _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} \ge \liminf _{n\to \infty } \exp \left( \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \log \left( \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} \right) \right) = e^{-\gamma /2}. \tag{2.22}\cssId{texmlid14}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} 1 \leq (M(f))^p \leq \|f\|_p^p \leq \|{\hat{f}}\|_p^p \le \||f| + 1/n\|_p^p \leq \|f\|_p^p + n^{-p}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} 1 \leq M(f) \leq \|f\|_p \leq \|{\hat{f}}\|_p \le \||f| + 1/n\|_p \leq \|f\|_p + n^{-1}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} 1 \leq \|{\hat{f}}\|_p/\| f\|_p \le (1 + n^{-p}+n^{-1} )^{1+1/p} \tag{2.23}\cssId{texmlid18}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty }{\underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}}{\frac {\| f\|_p}{\sqrt {n}}}}= \Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty }{\underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}}{\frac {\|{\hat{f}}\|_p}{\sqrt {n}}}} = \Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \limsup _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} \le \limsup _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \, \frac {\|{\hat{f}}\|_p}{\sqrt {n}} = \Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{p\to 0^+} \Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p} = \exp \left( \frac 12 \frac {\Gamma '(1)}{\Gamma (1)}\right) = e^{-\gamma /2}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \limsup _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} \leq e^{-\gamma /2}. \tag{2.24}\cssId{texmlid15}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \lim _{n\to \infty } \underset {f\in {\mathfrak{L}}_n}{\operatorname {mean}} \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} = e^{-\gamma /2}. \tag{2.25}\cssId{texmlid17}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lim _{n\to \infty } \frac {1}{2^n}\left| \left\{ f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n : \left| \frac {\| f \|_p}{\sqrt {n}} -\Gamma (1+p/2)^{1/p} \right| >\varepsilon \right\}\right| =0. \end{equation*} \]

\[ B_{n,\varepsilon } = \left\{f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n: \left| \left\| \frac {{\hat{f}}}{\sqrt {n}} \right\|_p - h_p \right| < \varepsilon , \hskip .5em\left| \frac {M({\hat{f}})}{\sqrt {n}} - h_0 \right| < \varepsilon \right\}.{} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray} \bigg ( \prod _{f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n \setminus B_{n,\varepsilon }} {(M({\hat{f}})/\sqrt {n})} \bigg )^{1/2^n} & = & \frac {\bigg ( \prod _{f \in {\mathfrak{L}}_n} {(M({\hat{f}})/\sqrt {n})} \bigg )^{1/2^n}} {\bigg ( \prod _{f \in B_{n,\varepsilon }} {(M({\hat{f}})/\sqrt {n})} \bigg )^{1/2^n}} \\ & \geq & \frac {h_0-\varepsilon }{(h_0+\varepsilon )^{m_{n,\varepsilon }}} \geq \frac {h_0-\varepsilon }{(h_0+\varepsilon )^{1-\varepsilon }} \tag{2.28}\cssId{texmlid21}{}{} \end{eqnarray} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \prod _{N/10 \leq j\leq N}(1-\cos (5j/N))^{-1/2} = \exp \left(-\frac 12 \sum _{N/10 \leq j\leq N} \log (1-\cos (5j/N)) \right) \tag{25}\cssId{texmlid13}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \phi (x):=-\log (1-\cos (5x/N)), \]

\[ \begin{equation} \sum _{N/10 \leq j\leq N} \phi (j)\!=\!\int _{\lfloor N/10 \rfloor }^{N+1} \phi (x)dx -\frac 12(\phi (N+1)-\phi (\lfloor N/10 \rfloor ))\!+\! \int _{\lfloor N/10 \rfloor }^{N+1}(\{x\}-\frac 12)\phi '(x)dx. \tag{26}\cssId{eq:euler}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \int _{\lfloor N/10 \rfloor }^{N+1} | \phi '(x) | dx &= \int _{ N/10 }^{N+1} | \phi '(x) | dx + O(1) \\ &= -\int _{ N/10 }^{\pi N/5}\phi '(x) dx + \int _{\pi N/5}^{N+1}\phi '(x)dx +O(1) \\ &= -2\phi (\pi N/5)+\phi (N/10)+\phi (N+1)+O(1) = O(1). \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \int \phi (x) dx = -\frac {5i x^2}{2N} + 2x \log (1-e^{5ix/N}) - x \log (1-\cos (5x/n)) - \frac 25 i N \mathrm{Li}_2(e^{5ix/N}). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \int _{\lfloor N/10 \rfloor }^{N+1} \phi (x)dx = -c N + O(1), \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} c = \frac {1}{40}(99 i +8\log (1-e^{i/2}) -80 \log (1-e^{5i}) -4\log (1-\cos (1/2)) \\ + 40 \log (1-\cos 5) -16i \mathrm{Li}_2(e^{i/2}) +16i \mathrm{Li}_2(e^{5i})) \approx 0.11262. \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \prod _{N/10 \leq j\leq N}(1-\cos (5j/N))^{-1/2} = \exp (-\tfrac 12 cN + O(1)), \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \prod _{N/10 \leq j\leq N} \frac {1}{|1-e^{z j/N}|} = O(2^{-9N/20} e^{-cN/2} (1+\varepsilon )^N ) = O(0.7^N). \tag{27}\cssId{texmlid17}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align*} 1+ e^{2j \Re (z)/N}& - 2\cos (5j/N) e^{j \Re (z)/N} \geq 1+\left[1+x+\frac {x^2}{2}+\frac {x^3}{6} \right]_{x=2j \Re (z)/N} \\ &- 2\left[1-\frac {x^2}{2}+\frac {x^4}{24} \right]_{x=5j/N} \cdot \left[1+x+\frac {x^2}{2} \right]_{x=j \Re (z)/N}. \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \geq \frac {11j^2}{12N^2}(\Re (z)^2+25). \tag{28}\cssId{texmlid15}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align} \prod _{1\leq j\leq N/10} \frac {1}{|1-e^{z j/N}|} &\leq \prod _{1\leq j\leq N/10} \sqrt {\frac {12}{11}} \frac {N}{j} ((\Re z)^2 +25)^{-1/2} \\ &\leq \left( \frac {12}{275} \right)^{N/20} N^{N/10} \lfloor N/10 \rfloor !^{-1}(1+\varepsilon )^N \\ & \leq \left( \left(\frac {12}{275}\right)^{1/20}(10e)^{1/10}(1+\varepsilon )\right)^N \leq 1.19^N, \tag{29}\cssId{texmlid18}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {(-1)^{l-1}}{N^l} \frac {1}{2i\pi } \int _{|z|=5} \mathbf{1}_{\{\Re z>0\}} F(z,N) dz = O(0.98^N). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \alpha (L) \leq c(L). \]

\[ F_L(a,z)=a^{-w(D)}\Lambda _D(a,z) \]

\[ \Lambda _{D_+}(a,z)+\Lambda _{D_-}(a,z)=z(\Lambda _{D_0}(a,z)+\Lambda _{D_\infty }(a,z)). \]

\[ a\,\Lambda _{D_+}(a,z)=\Lambda _D(a,z)=a^{-1}\Lambda _{D_-}(a,z). \]

\[ \Lambda _D(a,z) = \Lambda _{D_1}(a,z)\, \Lambda _{D_2}(a,z). \]

\[ \Lambda _D(a,z) = (z^{-1}a-1+z^{-1}a^{-1})\, \Lambda _{D_1}(a,z)\, \Lambda _{D_2}(a,z). \]

\[ \Lambda _D(a,z)=\sum _{i=m}^n f_i(z)a^i \]

\[ f_m(z)=\langle k_m z^{h_m}\rangle , \]

\[ f_n(z)=\langle k_n z^{h_n}\rangle , \]

\[ \sum _{i=m}^n f_i(z)a^i=\left[\langle k_n z^{h_n}\rangle a^{n},\langle k_m z^{h_m}\rangle a^{m}\right],\quad (m<n) \]

\[ z(z^2-1)a^{-1}+z^2a^{-2}-2za^{-3}=\left[\langle z^3\rangle a^{-1},\langle -2z\rangle a^{-3}\right]. \]

\[ \Lambda _{(-m,n)}= \begin{cases} \ \left[\langle z\rangle a^{k-1},\langle z^{k-1}\rangle a^{-1}\right] &\text{if } k=m-n>1, \\ \ a^{-1} &\text{if } k=m-n=1, \\ \ z^{-1}a-1+z^{-1}a^{-1} &\text{if } k=n-m=0, \\ \ a &\text{if } k=n-m=1, \\ \ \left[\langle z^{k-1}\rangle a,\langle z\rangle a^{-(k-1)}\right] &\text{if } k=n-m>1. \\ \end{cases} \]

\[ \sup _{(\alpha ,\beta )\in P \times Q}\, \sup _{(y,z)\in P\times Q}\, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus ( \Omega _1^*\cup \Omega _2^*)} \left|K(x,y,z)-K(x,\alpha ,\beta ) \right| \, dx \]

\[ \inf _{(\alpha ,\beta )\in P \times Q}\, \sup _{(y,z)\in P\times Q}\, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus ( \Omega _1^*\cup \Omega _2^*)} \left|K(x,y,z)-K(x,\alpha ,\beta ) \right| \, dx. \]

\[ \sum _{Q\in D_1} |Q| \, \int _{ \Omega _1} \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_Q,z)|\,dx \, dz \]

\[ \leq \sum _{Q\in D_1} |Q| \, \sum _{Q'\in D_1} |Q'| \, \sup _{z\in Q'} \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_Q,z)|\,dx\, \]

\[ \leq \sum _{(Q,Q')\in D_1\times D_1}\!\!|Q| \, |Q'|\! \sup _{(\alpha ,\beta )\in Q\times Q'}\, \sup _{(y,z)\in Q\times Q'} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus ( \Omega _1^* \cup \Omega _1^*)}\! \left|K(x,y,z)\!-\!K(x,\alpha ,\beta ) \right| dx \]

\[ \leq B\left( | \cup _{Q\in D_1} Q|+ |\cup _{Q'\in D_1} Q'| \right) \leq 2 B \sum _{Q\in D_1} |Q|. \]

\[ \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1} \, \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_Q,z)|\,dx \, dz\leq B. \]

\[ \sum _{Q\in D_1}|Q|\int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_Q,z)|\,dx \, dz \]

\[ \leq 2B \sum _{Q\in D_1}|Q|+ \sum _{Q\in D_1}|Q|\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1} \sup _{y\in Q}\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*}|K(x,y,z)-K(x,y_Q,z)|dx\,dz \]

\[ \leq 3B\sum _{Q\in D_1}|Q|. \]

\[ \int _{\mathbb{R}^n}\sup _{y\in Q}\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^*}|K(x,y,z)-K(x,y_Q,z)|dxdz \lesssim B, \]

\[ \int _0^1 \Phi (t)\,\frac {dt}{t}<\infty . \]

\[ |K(x,y,z)-K(x,y',z')|\leq \frac {C}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac {|y-y'|+ |z-z'| }{ |x-y|+|x-z| }\Big ) \]

\[ \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \, \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_Q,z)|\,dx\, dz \leq C \]

\[ \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \, \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _1^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_Q,z)|\,dx\, dz \]

\[ \lesssim \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \, \sup _{y\in Q} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac {|y-y_Q|}{ |x-y|+|x-z| }\Big ) \,dx \, dz \]

\[ \lesssim \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \frac {1}{ (|x-y_Q|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac {\sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q)}{ |x-y_Q|}\Big ) \,dx \, dz \]

\[ \lesssim \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \frac {1}{ |x-y_Q|^{n} } \Phi \Big (\frac { \sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q)}{ |x-y_Q|}\Big ) \,dx \]

\[ \lesssim \int _{|x|>c_n \ell (Q)} \frac {1}{ |x|^{n} } \Phi \Big (\frac {c_n \ell (Q)}{ |x|}\Big ) \,dx <\infty . \]

\[ \sup _{(y,z)\in P\times Q} \,\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (\Omega _1^{*} \cup \Omega _2^*)} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y_P, z_Q)|\,dx \]

\[ \lesssim \sup _{(y,z)\in P\times Q} \, \left(\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (P^\ast \cup Q^\ast )} \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac {|y-y_P|+ |z-z_Q| }{ |x-y|+|x-z| }\Big ) \,dx \right) \]

\[ \lesssim \sup _{(y,z)\in P\times Q} \, \left(\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (P^\ast \cup Q^\ast )} \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac { \sqrt {n}\, (\ell (P)+\ell (Q) )}{ |x-y_P|+|x-z_Q| }\Big ) \,dx \right) \]

\[ \lesssim \inf _{(y,z)\in P\times Q} \, \left(\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (P^\ast \cup Q^\ast )} \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac { \sqrt {n}\, (\ell (P)+\ell (Q)) }{ |x-y_P|+|x-z_Q| }\Big ) \,dx \right). \]

\[ \sum _{(P,Q)\in D_1\times D_2} |P| |Q| \,\sup _{(y,z)\in P\times Q}\,\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (\Omega _1^* \cup \Omega _2^*)} \left|K(x,y,z)-K(x,y_P,z_Q) \right| \, dx \]

\[ \lesssim \!\! \!\! \!\! \sum _{(P,Q)\in D_1\times D_2}\!\! \!\! \!\! \!\! |P| |Q|\, \inf _{(y,z)\in P\times Q} \, \left(\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (P^\ast \cup Q^\ast )} \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac { \sqrt {n}\, (\ell (P)+\ell (Q) )}{ |x-y_P|+|x-z_Q| }\Big ) \,dx \right) \]

\[ \lesssim \,\sum _{(P,Q)\in D_1\times D_2}\, \int _P \int _Q \, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (P^\ast \cup Q^\ast )} \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n} } \Phi \Big (\frac { \sqrt {n}\, (\ell (P)+\ell (Q) )}{ |x-y_P|+|x-z_Q| }\Big )\,dx \,dydz \]

\[ =C\,\left(\sum _{(P,Q)\in D_1\times D_2: \ell (P)\leq \ell (Q)}\, +\sum _{(P,Q)\in D_1\times D_2: \ell (Q)\leq \ell (P) } \right) = I + II. \]

\[ I \lesssim \,\sum _{(P,Q)\in D_1\times D_2}\, \int _P \int _Q \, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus (P^\ast \cup Q^\ast )} \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n}} \]

\[ \times \Phi \Big (\frac {2 \sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q) }{ |x-y_P|+|x-z_Q| }\Big )\,dx \,dydz \]

\[ \lesssim \,\sum _{Q\in D_2}\,\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \, \int _Q \,\sum _{P\in D_1}\, \int _P \, \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n}} \, \Phi \Big (\frac {2 \sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q) }{ |x-z_Q| }\Big ) \,dy \,dzdx \]

\[ \lesssim \,\sum _{Q\in D_2}\,\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \, \int _Q \, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \, \frac {1}{ (|x-y|+|x-z|)^{2n}} dy \,dz \, \Phi \Big (\frac {2 \sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q) }{ |x-z_Q| }\Big )\,dx. \]

\[ I\lesssim \, \,\sum _{Q\in D_2}\,\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \, \int _Q \, \frac {1}{|x-z|^{n}} \Phi \Big (\frac {2 \sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q) }{|x-z_Q| }\Big )dx\,dz \]

\[ \lesssim \, \,\sum _{Q\in D_2}\,\int _Q \,\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus Q^\ast } \, \frac {1}{|x-z|^{n}} \Phi \Big (\frac {2 \sqrt {n}\, \ell (Q) }{ |x-z_Q| }\Big )\,dx\,dz \]

\[ \begin{equation} |\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\,:\,|T(f_1,f_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2\}|\leq C \left(\int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \frac {|f_1(x)|}{\lambda } \, dx\right)^{1/2} \left(\int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \frac {|f_2(x)|}{\lambda } \, dx\right)^{1/2}, \tag{3.1}\cssId{mainestimate}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} |\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\,:\,|T(f_1,f_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2\}|\leq \frac {C}{\lambda }, \tag{3.2}\cssId{debilHormnader}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} |\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\,:\,|T(f_1,f_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2\}| &\leq & |\{x \notin {\Omega ^\ast }\,:\,|T(f_1,f_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2\}|+| {\Omega ^\ast }|\\ &\leq & |\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\,:\,|T(g_1,g_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2/4\}|\\ &+&|\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega ^\ast }\,:\,|T(g_1,b_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2/4\}|\\ &+&|\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega ^\ast }\,:\,|T(b_1,g_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2/4\}|\\ &+&|\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega ^\ast }\,:\,|T(b_1,b_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2/4\}|\\ &+&| {\Omega ^\ast }|\\ &=&|E_1|+|E_2|+|E_3|+|E_4|+| {\Omega ^\ast }|. \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \begin{split} |E_{2}|&\leq \frac {C}{\lambda ^2}\int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega ^*}} \sum _k |T(g_1,b_{ 2,k})(x)|\, dx\\ &\leq \frac {C}{\lambda ^2} \sum _k \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega ^*}} \left|\int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \int _{Q_{ 2,k}} K(x,y,z)g_1(y) b_{ 2,k}(z)\,dz\,dy\right|\, dx\\ &\leq \frac {C}{\lambda ^2}\sum _k \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega _2^*} \left|\int _{\mathbb{R}^n} g_1(y) \int _{Q_{ 2,k}} \left(K(x,y,z)-K(x,y,z_{Q_{ 2,k}})\right)\right.\\ &\qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \left.\vphantom {\int _{R}}\times b_{2,k}(z)\,dz\,dy\right|\, dx\\ &\leq \frac {C}{\lambda ^2} \sum _k \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} |g_1(y)| \int _{Q_{ 2,k}} |b_{ 2,k}(z)| \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega ^*} |K(x,y,z)-K(x,y,z_{Q_{2,k}})|\, dx\, dz\, dy\\ &\leq \frac {C}{\lambda ^2} \sum _k \int _{\mathbb{R}^n}\left( |g_1(y)| \int _{Q_{2,k}} |b_{ 2,k}(z)|\,dz\right.\\ &\qquad \qquad \qquad \qquad \left. \times \sup _{z\in Q_{2,k}} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega ^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y,z_{Q_{ 2,k}})|\,dx\right)dy\\ &\leq \frac {C}{\lambda } \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} |g_1(y)| \sum _k |Q_{2,k}| \sup _{z\in Q_{2,k}} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega ^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y,z_{Q_{2,k}})|\,dx\,dy\\ &\leq \frac {C}{\lambda } \|g_1\|_{\infty }\, \int _{\mathbb{R}^n} \sum _k |Q_{2,k}| \sup _{z\in Q_{2,k}} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus \Omega ^*} |K(x,y,z) -K(x,y,z_{Q_{2,k}})|\,dx\,dy \\ &\leq C |\Omega _2| \leq \frac {C}{\lambda }, \end{split} \end{equation*} \]

\[ |E_4|=|\{x\in \mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega }\,:\,|T(b_1,b_2)(x)|>\lambda ^2/4\}|. \]

\[ \begin{eqnarray*} |E_{4}|&\leq &\frac {C}{\lambda ^2}\sum _{l,k} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n\setminus {\Omega ^*}}| T(b_{ 1,l},b_{ 2,k})(x)|\, dx\\ &\leq &\frac {C}{\lambda ^2}\sum _{l,k} \int _{\mathbb{R}^n \setminus \Omega ^*} \left|\int _{Q_{ 1,l}}\int _{Q_{ 2,k}} K(x,y,z) b_{ 1,l}(y) b_{ 2,k}(z)\,dzdy\right|\, dx.\\ \end{eqnarray*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left|\theta (u_{i,j})\right| = \left|u_{i,j}\right| > n \qquad \text{and}\qquad \left|a_{i,j} \cdot g_i\right| \ge \left|a_{i,j}\right| \ge n. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \psi (\theta (u_{i,j}) \cdot (a_{i,j} \cdot g_i)) = \psi (\theta (u_{i,j})) \cdot \psi (a_{i,j} \cdot g_i). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{align} m' = \psi (m) & = \psi \Big ( \sum _{i,j} \theta (u_{i,j}) \cdot (a_{i,j} \cdot g_i) \Big )\\ & = \sum _{i,j} \psi (\theta (u_{i,j})) \cdot \psi (a_{i,j} \cdot g_i)\\ & = \sum _{i,j} \theta '(\phi (u_{i,j})) \cdot \psi (a_{i,j} \cdot g_i). \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left|\psi (a_{i,j} \cdot g_i)\right| = \left|a_{i,j} \cdot g_i\right| = \left|a_{i,j}\right| + \left|g_i\right| \le b_R + b_M \le b, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lambda := \Big (\sum _{\ell = 1}^L \|a(\tau _{j_\ell })\|_H^p\Big )^\frac {1}{p} \leq \Big (\sum _{k = 1}^K \|\phi _{k-1}\|_H^p\Big )^\frac {1}{p} = 1. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} b = \sum _{\ell = 1}^L \frac {a(\tau _{j_\ell } )}{\lambda } \chi _{[\tau _{j_\ell }, \tau _{j_{\ell +1}})}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{align} \| u_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} = \bigg \|\sum _{j = 1}^\infty \lambda _j \cdot (a_j)_{\mathcal{P}}\bigg \|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \leq \sum _{j = 1}^\infty |\lambda _j| \|(a_j)_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \leq \sum _{j = 1}^\infty |\lambda _j| . \tag{A.10}\cssId{U3c}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|u - u_J\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \leq \sum _{j = J+1}^\infty |\lambda _j| < \frac {\varepsilon }{2}. \tag{A.11}\cssId{U3d}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \| u - u_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} & \leq \| u - u_J\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} +\| u_J -( u_J)_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} + \|( u - u_J)_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})}\\ & < \frac {\varepsilon }{2} + 0 + \frac {\varepsilon }{2} = \varepsilon . \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|u \|_{U^p([a, t_* - \delta _n))} < \|u \|_{U^p([a, t_* ))} - \varepsilon . \tag{A.12}\cssId{U4a0}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|v_\delta \|_{U^p(\mathbb{R}) }\leq \|u \|_{U^p([a, t_* - \delta ))} + \frac {\varepsilon }{4}. \tag{A.13}\cssId{U4a1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align} v_\delta = \sum _{j = 1}^\infty \lambda _j^\delta a_j^\delta = \sum _{j = 1}^\infty \lambda _j^\delta \sum _{k = 1}^{K_j^\delta } \phi _{k-1}^{\delta , j} \chi _{[t^{\delta , j}_{k-1}, t^{\delta , j}_k)} , \tag{A.14}\cssId{U4a}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|v_\delta \|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} = \|\widetilde{v}_\delta \|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})}. \tag{A.15}\cssId{U4a2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align} \| u \|_{U^p([a, t_*))} \leq \|\widetilde{v}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \leq \|\widetilde{v}_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} + \frac {\varepsilon }{8}. \tag{A.16}\cssId{U4b}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} \| u(t_1) - u(t_2) \|_H < \frac {\varepsilon }{8 \cdot (\#\mathcal{P}+1)} \tag{A.17}\cssId{U4c}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \widetilde{v}_{\mathcal{P}} - (\widetilde{v}_\delta )_{\mathcal{P}} & = \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}\tau _j \in \mathcal{P}\\ \tau _j > t_* - \delta \end{subarray}} \big ( u (\tau _j) - u (t_* - \delta )\big )\chi _{[\tau _j, \tau _{j+1})}\\ & = \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}\tau _j \in \mathcal{P}\\ \tau _j \in ( t_* - \delta , t_*) \end{subarray}} \big ( u (\tau _j) - u (t_* - \delta )\big )\chi _{[\tau _j, \tau _{j+1})} + \big (u(t_*) - u(t_* - \delta ) \big )\chi _{[t_*, \infty )}. \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{align} \| \widetilde{v}_{\mathcal{P}} - (\widetilde{v}_\delta )_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} & \leq \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}\tau _j \in \mathcal{P}\\ \tau _j \in ( t_* - \delta , t_*) \end{subarray}} \| u (\tau _j) - u (t_* - \delta )\|_{H} + \| u(t_*) - u(t_* - \delta )\|_H \\ & < \frac {\varepsilon }{8} \tag{A.18}\cssId{U4d}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \| u \|_{U^p([a, t_*))} & \leq \|(\widetilde{v}_{\delta _n})_{\mathcal{P}}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} + \frac {\varepsilon }{4} \leq \|\widetilde{v}_{\delta _n}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} + \frac {\varepsilon }{4} \leq \|u \|_{U^p([a, t_* - \delta _n))} + \frac {\varepsilon }{2}\\ & \leq \|u \|_{U^p([a, t_*))} - \frac {\varepsilon }{2} \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{align} \|\widetilde{v}_0\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \leq \|u \|_{U^p([a, t_*))} + \frac {\varepsilon }{4}. \tag{A.19}\cssId{U5b}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} \sum _{j = J+1}^\infty |\lambda _j| < \frac {\varepsilon }{4}. \tag{A.20}\cssId{U5c}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lambda _0 := \|w_J(t_*)\|_H, \quad \phi := \lambda _0^{-1} w_J(t_*), \quad \text{and} \quad a_0 := \chi _{[t_*, \infty )} \phi . \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{align} \| \widetilde{w}\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \leq |\lambda _0| + \sum _{j = J+1}^\infty |\lambda _j| < \frac { \varepsilon }{2}, \tag{A.21}\cssId{U5d}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \lambda _0 = \bigg \| w(t_*) - \sum _{j = J+1}^\infty \lambda _j a_j(t_*)\bigg \|_H =\bigg \|\sum _{j = J+1}^\infty \lambda _j a_j(t_*)\bigg \|_H \leq \sum _{j = J+1}^\infty |\lambda _j| < \frac {\varepsilon }{4}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \| u \|_{U^p([a, t_*+\delta ))} & \leq \| \widetilde{v}_0\|_{U^p([a, t_*+\delta ))} + \|\widetilde{w} \|_{U^p([a, t_*+\delta ))} \leq \| \widetilde{v}_0\|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} + \| \widetilde{w} \|_{U^p(\mathbb{R})} \\ & \leq \| u \|_{U^p([a, t_*))} +\frac 34 \varepsilon \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{align} \|u \|_{X^s([a, t))} = \|u\cdot \chi _{[a, t)}\|_{X^s(\mathbb{R})}. \tag{A.22}\cssId{UP0}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} \|u \|_{X^s([a, t))} \leq \| v\|_{X^s(\mathbb{R})}. \tag{A.23}\cssId{UP1}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} \|u\cdot \chi _{[a, t)} \|_{X^s(\mathbb{R})} = \|v\cdot \chi _{[a, t)} \|_{X^s(\mathbb{R})} \leq \| v\|_{X^s(\mathbb{R})}. \tag{A.24}\cssId{UP2}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} \|u \|_{X^s([a, t))} & = \|u\cdot \chi _{[a, t)}\|_{X^s(\mathbb{R})} = \bigg (\sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}N\geq 1\\ \text{dyadic} \end{subarray}} N^{2s} \|\mathbf{P}_N u \cdot \chi _{[a, t)} \|^2_{U^2_\Delta (\mathbb{R}; L^2)}\bigg )^\frac {1}{2} \\ & = \bigg (\sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}N\geq 1\\ \text{dyadic} \end{subarray}} N^{2s} \|\mathbf{P}_N u \|^2_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t); L^2)}\bigg )^\frac {1}{2}, \tag{A.25}\cssId{UP3}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \bigg (\sum _{j = J}^\infty 2^{2js} \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} v \|^2_{U^2_\Delta (\mathbb{R}; L^2)}\bigg )^\frac {1}{2}<\frac {\varepsilon }{4}. \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{align} \bigg (\sum _{j = J}^\infty 2^{2js} \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|^2_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t); L^2)}\bigg )^\frac {1}{2}<\frac {\varepsilon }{4} \tag{A.26}\cssId{UP4}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} 2^{js}\Big | \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t_*); L^2)} - \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t_*+\delta ); L^2)} \Big | < \frac \varepsilon {2 J^\frac {1}{2}} \tag{A.27}\cssId{UP5}{}{} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align*} \Big |\| u \|_{X^s([a, t_*))} & - \| u \|_{X^s([a, t_*+\delta ))} \Big |\\ &\leq \bigg (\sum _{j = 0}^\infty 2^{2js} \big (\|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t_*); L^2)} - \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t_*+\delta ); L^2)}\big )^2 \bigg )^\frac {1}{2}\\ & \leq J^\frac {1}{2} \max _{j = 0, \dotsc , J-1} 2^{js}\Big | \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t_*); L^2)} - \|\mathbf{P}_{2^j} u \|_{U^2_\Delta ([a, t_*+\delta ); L^2)} \Big | +\frac {\varepsilon }{2}\\ & < \varepsilon \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \hat{a}, \hat{\sigma }= \left\{ \begin{array}{cl} a, \sigma & \mbox{ in } B_{\gamma r_2} \setminus B_{r_2}, \\[6.0pt] I, 1 & \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{\gamma r_2}. \end{array} \right. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} - F^{-1}_*\hat{a}, - F^{-1}_*\hat{\sigma }, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} F(x) = \frac {r_2^2}{|x|^2} x. \tag{1.1}\cssId{def-F}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} T_*\hat{a} (y) = \frac {D T (x) \hat{a}(x) D T (x)^T}{J(x)} \quad \mbox{ and } \quad T_* \hat{\sigma }(y) = \frac {\hat{\sigma }(x)}{J(x)}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} r_1 = r_2^2/ r_3. \tag{1.2}\cssId{cond-r}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \Big (r_3^2/r_2^2 \Big )^{d-2} I, \Big (r_3^2/r_2^2 \Big )^{d}. \tag{1.3}\cssId{choice-A}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} A, \Sigma = \left\{ \begin{array}{cl} \hat{a}, \hat{\sigma }& \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{r_2}, \\[6.0pt] F^{-1}_*\hat{a}, F^{-1}_* \hat{\sigma }& \mbox{ in } B_{r_2} \setminus B_{r_1}, \\[6.0pt] \Big (r_3^2/r_2^2 \Big )^{d-2} I, \Big (r_3^2/r_2^2 \Big )^{d} & \mbox{ in } B_{r_1},\\[6.0pt] I, 1 & \mbox{ otherwise}, \end{array} \right. \tag{1.4}\cssId{defA}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} s_\delta : = \left\{ \begin{array}{cl} -1 + i \delta & \mbox{ in } B_{r_2} \setminus B_{r_1}, \\[6.0pt] 1 & \mbox{ otherwise}. \end{array} \right. \tag{1.5}\cssId{def-ss}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \frac {1}{\Lambda } |\xi |^{2} \le a (x) \xi \cdot \xi \le \Lambda |\xi |^{2} \quad \forall \, \xi \in \mathbb{R}^{d}, \mbox{ for a.e. } x \in B_{\gamma r_{2}} \setminus B_{r_2}, \tag{1.6}\cssId{cond-a}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \hat{a} \, \mbox{is Lipschitz in}\, B_{r_3} \setminus B_{r_2}. \tag{1.7} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} G(x) = r_{3}^{2} x/ |x|^{2}. \tag{1.8}\cssId{def-G}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} G_{*} F_{*} A = I \ \text{and } G_*F_*1=1\mbox{ in } B_{r_{3}}, \tag{1.9}\cssId{GF}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} {\mathrm{div}}(s_\delta A \nabla u_\delta ) + s_0 k^2 \Sigma u_\delta = f \mbox{ in } \Omega , \tag{1.10}\cssId{eq-uu-delta}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \Delta u + k^2 u = f \mbox{ in } \Omega . \tag{1.11}\cssId{eq-uu}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \mbox{equation}\, (1.11)\, \mbox{with } f = 0 \mbox{ has only a zero solution in}\, H^1_0(\Omega ). \tag{1.12} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} u_{\delta } \to u \mbox{ weakly in } H^{1} (\Omega \setminus B_{r_3}) \mbox{ as } \delta \to 0. \tag{1.13}\cssId{key-point}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|v\|_{L^{\infty }(\partial B_{R_2})} \leq \|v\|_{L^{\infty }(\partial B_{R_1})}^{\alpha } \|v\|_{L^{\infty }(\partial B_{r_3})}^{1 - \alpha }, \tag{2.1}\cssId{Hadamard}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \displaystyle \alpha = \log \Big ( \frac {R_3}{R_2} \Big ) \Big / \log \Big (\frac {R_3}{R_1} \Big ). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \operatorname {div}(M \nabla v) + \vec{b} \cdot \nabla v + c v = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{R_3}, \tag{2.2}\cssId{Equation}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|v\|_{L^{\infty }(\partial B_{R_2})} \leq C \|v\|_{L^{\infty }(\partial B_{R_1})}^{\alpha } \|v\|_{L^{\infty }(\partial B_{r_3})}^{1 - \alpha }, \tag{2.3}\cssId{Landis}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|v\|_{L^{2}(\partial B_{R_2})} \leq C \|v\|_{L^{2}(\partial B_{R_1})}^{\alpha } \|v\|_{L^2(\partial B_{r_3})}^{1 - \alpha } \tag{2.4}\cssId{Lin}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \Delta v + k^2 v = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{R_3}. \tag{2.5}\cssId{H}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_r)} = \| v\|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_r)} + \| M \nabla v \cdot \nu \|_{H^{-1/2}(\partial B_r)}. \tag{2.6}\cssId{H-norm}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} |{\mathrm{div}}(M \nabla v)| \le c_1 |\nabla v| + c_2|v|, \quad \mbox{ in } {B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}. \tag{2.7}\cssId{eq-Main}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_2})} \le C\| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})} ^{\alpha } \| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})}^{1-\alpha }, \quad \mbox{ where } \quad \alpha := \frac {R_2^{-q} - R_3^{-q}}{R_1^{-q} - R_{3}^{-q}}. \tag{2.8}\cssId{def-alpha}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {1}{\Lambda } |\xi |^2 \le M(x) \xi \cdot \xi \le \Lambda |\xi |^2 \quad \forall \, \xi \in \mathbb{R}^d, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} L : = \| M \|_{L^\infty } + R_3\|\nabla M \|_{L^\infty }. \tag{2.9}\cssId{def-L1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}(x \cdot M \nabla z) \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla z) \ge - \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} C L^2|\nabla z|^2 - \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} C L^2 r |\nabla z|^2, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{multline} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}(x \cdot M \nabla z) \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla z) = - \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} \nabla ( x \cdot M \nabla z) \cdot M\nabla z \tag{2.10}\cssId{texmlid3}{}{}\\ + \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} (x \cdot M\nabla z) \, M \nabla z \cdot \nu . \end{multline} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \begin{split} \frac {\partial }{\partial x_i}(x \cdot M\nabla z) &= \frac {\partial }{\partial x_i} \Big ( M_{k j} x_j \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_k} \Big )\\ & = M_{k j} x_j \frac {\partial ^2 z}{\partial x_i \partial x_k} + M_{k i } \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_k} + x _j \frac {\partial M_{k j}}{\partial x_i} \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_k} \end{split}\tag{2.11}\cssId{texmlid1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{multline} -\int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} 2 x_j M_{kj} \frac {\partial ^2 z}{\partial x_i \partial x_k}M_{il} \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_l} = - \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}x_j M_{kj} M_{il} \frac {\partial }{\partial x_k}\left(\frac {\partial z}{\partial x_i} \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_l}\right) \tag{2.12}\cssId{texmlid2}{}{}\\ = \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {\partial (x_j M_{kj} M_{il})}{\partial x_k}\frac {\partial z}{\partial x_i} \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_l} - \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} x_j M_{kj} M_{il}\frac {\partial z}{\partial x_i} \frac {\partial z}{\partial x_l} \nu _k. \end{multline} \]

\[ \begin{equation} - \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} \nabla ( x \cdot M\nabla z) \cdot M\nabla z \ge - \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} C L^2|\nabla z|^2 - \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} C L^2 r|\nabla z|^2. \tag{2.13}\cssId{texmlid4}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{\beta r^{-p}} (M x \cdot \nabla |z|^2) \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla e^{-\beta r^{-p}}) + \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} C L^2 p^2 \beta ^2 r^{- 2 p-1} |z|^2 \\ [6.0pt] \ge \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {1}{2}\Lambda ^{-2} p^3 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2}|z|^2 - \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}C L^2 |\nabla z|^2, \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{align*} {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla e^{-\beta r^{-p}})& = p \beta e^{-\beta r^{-p}}\big [p \beta r^{-2 p - 4} - ( p + 2) r^{-p - 4}\big ] x\\ &\quad \cdot Mx +p \beta r^{-p - 2} e^{-\beta r^{-p}}\, {\mathrm{div}}(Mx). \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{\beta r^{-p}} (M x \cdot \nabla |z|^2) \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla e^{-\beta r^{-p}}) = P + Q. \tag{2.14}\cssId{texmlid7}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} P = P_1 + P_2 + P_3 \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left\{ \begin{array}{rl}\displaystyle P_1 &= \displaystyle - \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} p^2 \beta ^2 |z|^2 {\mathrm{div}}\big [ r^{- 2 p - 4} (x \cdot M x) M x \big ], \\[6.0pt] \displaystyle P_2 &= \displaystyle \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} p \beta (p+2) |z|^2 {\mathrm{div}}\big [ r^{- p - 4} (x \cdot M x) M x \big ], \\[6.0pt] \displaystyle P_3 &= \displaystyle \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} 2 p \beta r^{-p -2} {\mathrm{div}}(M x) z \nabla z \cdot Mx, \end{array}\right. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} Q = \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} p \beta |z|^2 \Big ( \big [p \beta r^{- 2p - 4} -( p + 2) r^{-p - 4} \big ] x \cdot M x \Big ) M x \cdot \nu . \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} - {\mathrm{div}}\big [ r^{- 2 p - 4} (x \cdot M x) M x \big ] = (2p + 4) (x \cdot Mx)^2 r^{-2p - 6} - r^{-2p - 4} {\mathrm{div}}\big [ (x \cdot Mx) Mx\big ]. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} P_1 \ge \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2}|z|^2 \big [ (2p + 4)\Lambda ^{-2} - C L^2 \big ] . \tag{2.15}\cssId{R1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} P_2 \ge - \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}(p + 2) p |\beta | r^{-p - 2}|z|^2 \big [ (p + 4)\Lambda ^{-2} + C L^2 \big ]. \tag{2.16}\cssId{R2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} P_1 + P_2 \ge \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\Lambda ^{-2} p^3 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2}|z|^2. \tag{2.17}\cssId{R12}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{align*} |P_3| \leq \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2} L^2 |z|^2 + \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} C L^2 |\nabla z|^2. \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{align} P &\geq \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {1}{2} p^3\beta ^2 \Lambda ^{-2} r^{-2p - 2}|z|^2 - \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} C L^2 |\nabla z|^2, \tag{2.18} \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} |Q| \le \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} 2 \Lambda ^2 p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2p -1 } |z|^2, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {r^{p + 2}e^{2\beta r^{-p}}}{2p |\beta |}\big [{\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v)\big ]^2 + \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} C L^2 e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |\nabla v|^2 \\ + \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} CL^2 p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2p-1} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}}|v|^2 + \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} C L^2 r e^{2 \beta r^{-p}}|\nabla v|^2 \\ \ge \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {1}{2} \Lambda ^{-2} p^3 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |v|^2, \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} z = e^{\beta r^{-p}} v \quad \mbox{ equivalently } v = e^{-\beta r^{-p}} z. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{align*} {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v) = 2\beta p r^{-p - 2} e^{-\beta r^{-p}} x \cdot M\nabla z + e^{-\beta r^{-p}} {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla z) + z {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla e^{-\beta r^{-p}}). \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{align*} &\frac {1}{2 }\big [ {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v) \big ]^2\\ &\qquad \ge 2|\beta | p r^{-p - 2} e^{-\beta r^{-p}} (x \cdot M\nabla z) \Big ( e^{-\beta r^{-p}} {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla z) + z {\mathrm{div}}( M\nabla e^{-\beta r^{-p}})\Big ). \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {r^{p + 2}e^{2\beta r^{-p}}}{2p|\beta |}\big [{\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v)\big ]^2 \geq \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}2 (x \cdot M\nabla z ) \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla z) \\ + \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{\beta r^{-p}} (Mx \cdot \nabla |z|^2) \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla e^{-\beta r^{-p}}). \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{multline} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {r^{p + 2}e^{2\beta r^{-p}}}{2p|\beta |}\big [{\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v)\big ]^2\tag{2.19}\cssId{p1-Lem3}{}{}\\ \ge \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\Big ( \Lambda ^{-2} p^3 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2}|z|^2 - C L^2 |\nabla z|^2 \Big ) \\ [6.0pt] - \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} \Big ( C L^2 p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2 p-1} |z|^2 + C L^2 r |\nabla z|^2 \Big ). \end{multline} \]

\[ \begin{equation} |\nabla z|^2 \leq 2 e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} (|\nabla v|^2 + p^2\beta ^2 r^{-2 p - 2}|v|^2). \tag{2.20}\cssId{p2-Lem3}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {r^{p + 2}e^{2\beta r^{-p}}}{2p|\beta |}\big [{\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v)\big ]^2\\ \ge \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} \left( \frac {1}{2} \Lambda ^{-2} p^3 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2} |v|^2 - C L^2 |\nabla v|^2 \right) \\ [6.0pt]- \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} \left( C L^2 p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2p-1} |v|^2 + C L^2 r |\nabla v|^2 \right). \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v) + \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |\nabla v|^2 \\ \le \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}C \beta ^2 p^2 r^{-2p - 2} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |v|^2+ \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} C e^{2\beta r^{-p}} (r|\nabla v|^2 + r^{-1}|v|^2), \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \begin{split} &- \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v)\\ &\qquad = \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}M\nabla v \cdot \nabla (e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v) - \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v M \nabla v \cdot \nu . \end{split}\tag{2.21}\cssId{s1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \begin{split} & \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}M\nabla v \cdot \nabla (e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v)\\ &\qquad =\int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\Big (e^{2\beta r^{-p}} M\nabla v \cdot \nabla v - 2 \beta p r^{-p - 2}e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v M\nabla v \cdot x \Big ) \end{split}\tag{2.22}\cssId{s2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v M \nabla v \cdot \nu \le \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} e^{2\beta r^{-p}} (r|\nabla v|^2 + L^2 r^{-1}|v|^2). \tag{2.23}\cssId{s3}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} 2 \beta p r^{-p - 2}v M\nabla v \cdot x \le \frac {1}{2} \Lambda ^{-1} |\nabla v|^2 + 8 \beta ^2 p^2 L^2 \Lambda r^{-2p - 2} |v|^2, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{multline*} \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}e^{2\beta r^{-p}} v \, {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v) + \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}\frac {1}{2} \Lambda ^{-1} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |\nabla v|^2 \\ \le \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}C \beta ^2 p^2 r^{-2p - 2} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |v|^2+ \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} C e^{2\beta r^{-p}} \big (r|\nabla v|^2 + r^{-1}|v|^2 \big ). \end{multline*} \]

\[ \begin{multline} \int _{{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}} e^{2\beta r^{-p}}|\beta | p \Big (p^3 \beta ^2 r^{-2p - 2} e^{2 \beta r^{-p}} |v|^2 + |\nabla v|^2 \Big )\tag{2.24}\cssId{comb}{}{}\\ \leq C \int _{B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}r^{p+2} e^{2\beta r^{-p}}|{\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla v)|^2 \\ + C \int _{\partial ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}})} |\beta | p e^{2\beta r^{-p}} \big (r|\nabla v|^2 + p^2 \beta ^2 r^{-2p -1}|v|^2 \big ), \end{multline} \]

\[ \begin{align*} |v \operatorname {div}(M \nabla v)| \le p|\beta |^2 |v|^2 r^{- 2p -2 } + \frac {4 }{p |\beta |} |\operatorname {div}(M \nabla v)|^2 r^{p+2}. \end{align*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} 1 < \lambda < \lambda _0 \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} D = B_{{\lambda R_3}} \setminus \overline B_{{R_1/\lambda }}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left\{ \begin{array}{cl} {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla u_1) = 0 &\mbox{in } D \setminus \partial B_{R_1},\\[6.0pt] \displaystyle [u_1] = v; \; \displaystyle [M\nabla u_1 \cdot \nu ] = M\nabla v \cdot \nu &\mbox{on } \partial B_{R_1},\\[6.0pt] u_1 = 0 &\mbox{on } \partial D, \end{array} \right. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left\{ \begin{array}{cl} {\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla u_3) = 0 &\mbox{in } D \setminus B_{R_3},\\[6.0pt] \displaystyle [u_3] = v; \; \displaystyle [M\nabla u_3 \cdot \nu ] = M\nabla v \cdot \nu &\mbox{on } \partial B_{R_3},\\[6.0pt] u_3 = 0 &\mbox{on } \partial D. \end{array} \right. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_1 \|_{H^1(D\setminus \partial B_{R_1} )} \le C \|v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})}, \quad \|u_1\|_{H^{3/2}(\partial B_{R_1/\gamma })} \leq C\|v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})} \tag{2.25}\cssId{inf-R1-Thm1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_3 \|_{H^1(D \setminus \partial B_{R_3})} \le C \|v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})}, \quad \|u_3\|_{H^{3/2}(\partial B_{\gamma R_3})} \leq C\|v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})}. \tag{2.26}\cssId{inf-R3-Thm1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} d_1 = (\lambda -1)R_1 \quad \mbox{ and } \quad d_3 = (\lambda - 1)R_3/\lambda . \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \varphi _1 = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} 1 & \mbox{ in } B_{R_1 + d_1/3} \setminus B_{R_1}, \\[6.0pt] 0 &\mbox{in } \mathbb{R}^d \setminus (B_{R_1 + d_1/2} \setminus B_{R_1/\lambda }), \end{array}\right. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \varphi _3 = \left\{ \begin{array}{ll} 1 &\mbox{in } B_{R_3} \setminus B_{R_3-d_3/3},\\[6.0pt] 0 &\mbox{in } \mathbb{R}^d \setminus (B_{\lambda R_3} \setminus B_{R_3 - d_3/2}). \end{array} \right. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} V = \left\{\begin{array}{cl} v- \varphi _1 u_1 - \varphi _3 u_3 & \mbox{ in } {B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}, \\[6.0pt] - \varphi _1 u_1 - \varphi _3 u_3 & \mbox{ in } D \setminus ({B_{R_3}\setminus \overline B_{R_1}}). \end{array}\right. \tag{2.27}\cssId{def-V-Thm1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \begin{split} & C \int _{D} e^{2\beta r^{-p}}\beta (\beta ^2 |V|^2 + |\nabla V|^2)\\ &\qquad \leq \int _{D} e^{2\beta r^{-p}}|{\mathrm{div}}(M\nabla V)|^2 + \int _{\partial D} |\beta | e^{2\beta r^{-p}} (|\nabla V|^2 + \beta ^2 |V|^2). \end{split}\tag{2.28}\cssId{texmlid5}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} C \int _{D} e^{2\beta r^{-p}}(|V|^2 + |\nabla V|^2) \leq \beta ^2 e^{2\beta \hat{R}_{3}^{-p}} \| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})}^2 + \beta ^2 e^{2\beta \hat{R}_{1}^{-p}} \|v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})}^2, \tag{2.29}\cssId{texmlid8}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \hat{R}_3 = R_3/ \lambda \quad \mbox{ and } \quad \hat{R}_1 = R_1 / \lambda . \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} C \|v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_2})} \leq \beta e^{\beta (\hat{R}_3^{-p} - R_2^{-p})} \| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})} + \beta e^{\beta (\hat{R}_1^{-p} - R_2^{-p})} \|v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})}. \tag{2.30}\cssId{point-point}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \alpha ' = \frac {R_2^{-p} - \hat{R}_3^{-p}}{\hat{R}_1^{-p} - \hat{R}_3^{-p}} \quad \mbox{ and }\quad \beta (R_2^{-p} - \hat{R}_1^{-p}) = (1 - \alpha ') \ln \Big (\|v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})} \big /\| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})} \Big ).3

Here we assume that \$\| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})} \neq 0\$ since otherwise \$v= 0\$. This fact is a consequence of the unique continuation principle and can be obtained from (2.30) by letting \$\beta \to \infty \$.

\end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_2})} \le C \beta \|v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})}^{\alpha '}\| v\|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_3})}^{1-\alpha '}. \tag{2.31}\cssId{texmlid6}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \alpha : = \frac {R_2^{-2p} - R_3^{-2p}}{R_1^{-2p} - R_3^{-2p}}. \tag{2.32}\cssId{alpha}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \alpha < \alpha ' \quad \forall R_2 \in (\gamma _0 R_1, R_3/ \gamma _0). \tag{2.33}\cssId{LL}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_2})} \le C \|v \|_{{\mathbf{H}}(\partial B_{R_1})}^{\alpha }\| v\|_{H(\partial B_{R_3})}^{1-\alpha }. \tag{2.34}\cssId{texmlid9}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} K(x) = R_2^2 x/ |x|^2. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \operatorname {div}(a \nabla v) + k^2 \sigma v = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{{R_3}} \setminus \overline B_{{R_2}} \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \operatorname {div}(K_*a \nabla w) + k^2 K_* \sigma w = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{{R_2}} \setminus \overline B_{{R_1}}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} w = v \quad \mbox{ and } \quad K_*a \nabla w \cdot \nu = - a \nabla v \cdot \nu \mbox{ on } \partial B_{R_2}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}^2 \le C \left(\delta ^{-1} \|f\|_{L^2(\Omega )}\|u_{\delta }\|_{L^2({\operatorname {supp}} f)} + \|f\|_{L^2(\Omega )}^2\right), \tag{3.1}\cssId{est-stability}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_n\|_{H^1(\Omega )} =1 \mbox{ and } \frac {1}{\delta _n} \|f_n\|_{L^2(\Omega )} \| u_n\|_{L^2({\operatorname {supp}} f_n)} + \| f_n\|_{L^2(\Omega )}^2 \to 0, \tag{3.2}\cssId{contradict-assumption}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \operatorname {div}(s_{\delta _n} A \nabla u_n) + k^2 s_0 \Sigma u_n= f_n \mbox{ in } \Omega . \tag{3.3}\cssId{eq-v-delta}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \operatorname {div}(s_0 A \nabla u) + k^2 s_0 \Sigma u = 0 \mbox{ in } \Omega . \tag{3.4}\cssId{eq-uu-1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \int _{\Omega } s_{\delta _n} A \nabla u_n \cdot \nabla \bar{u}_n \, dx - \int _{\Omega } k^2 s_0 \Sigma |u_n|^2 \, dx = - \int _\Omega f_n \bar{u}_n \, dx. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \frac {1}{\delta _n}\Big | \int _\Omega f_n \bar{u}_n \Big | \le \frac {1}{\delta }\|f_n \|_{L^2(\Omega )} \| u_n\|_{L^2({\operatorname {supp}} f_n)} \to 0 \mbox{ as $n \to \infty $ by }(3.2), \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| \nabla u_n\|_{L^2(B_{{r_2}} \setminus \overline B_{{r_1}})} \to 0 \mbox{ as } n \to \infty . \tag{3.5}\cssId{toto1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_n \|_{L^{2}(B_{r_2} \setminus B_{r_1})} \to 0 \mbox{ as } n \to \infty . \tag{3.6}\cssId{toto1-1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_n \|_{H^{1}(B_{r_2} \setminus B_{r_1})} \to 0 \mbox{ as } n \to \infty . \tag{3.7}\cssId{part-1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} u= 0 \mbox{ in } B_{r_2} \setminus B_{r_1} \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \begin{split} \| u_n \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r_2})} & + \| u_n \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r_1})} + \| A \nabla u_n \cdot \nu \|_{H^{-1/2}(\partial B_{r_2})}\\ & + \| A \nabla u_n \cdot \nu \|_{H^{-1/2}(\partial B_{r_1})} \to 0 \mbox{ as }n \to \infty . \end{split}\tag{3.8}\cssId{limit-1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} u_n \to 0 \mbox{ in } L^2(\Omega ) \mbox{ as } n \to \infty . \tag{3.9}\cssId{u0}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \int _{\Omega \setminus B_{r_2}} A \nabla u_n \cdot \nabla \bar{u}_n \, dx - \int _{\Omega \setminus B_{r_2}} k^2 s_0 \Sigma |u_n|^2 \, dx = - \int _\Omega f_n \bar{u}_n \, dx + \int _{\partial B_{r_2}} A \nabla u_n \cdot \nu \; \bar{u}_n. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|\nabla u_n \|_{L^2(\Omega \setminus B_{r_2})} \to 0 \mbox{ as } n \to \infty . \tag{3.10}\cssId{part-2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|\nabla u_n \|_{L^2(B_{r_1})} \to 0 \mbox{ as } n \to \infty . \tag{3.11}\cssId{part-3}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \|u_n \|_{H^1(\Omega )} \to 0 \mbox{ as } n \to \infty , \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_{\delta } \|_{H^{1}(\Omega )}^2 \le C \Big ( \delta ^{-1} \| f\|_{L^2(\Omega )} \|u_{\delta } \|_{L^2(\Omega \setminus B_{r_3})} + \| f\|_{L^2(\Omega )}^2 \Big ). \tag{3.12}\cssId{haha0}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} u_{1, \delta } = u_{\delta } \circ F^{-1} \mbox{ in } \mathbb{R}^{d} \setminus \bar{B}_{r_{2}}, \tag{3.13}\cssId{def-u1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} u_{2, \delta } = u_{1, \delta } \circ G^{-1} \mbox{ in } B_{r_{3}}. \tag{3.14}\cssId{def-u2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \operatorname {div}(A \nabla u_{1, \delta }) + \frac {1}{1- i \delta } k^2 \Sigma u_{1, \delta } = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{r_2}, \tag{3.15}\cssId{eqn-u1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \Delta u_{2, \delta } + k^2 u_{2, \delta } = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{r_3}. \tag{3.16}\cssId{eqn-u2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} u_{1, \delta } = u_{\delta } \Big |_{+} \mbox{ on } \partial B_{r_{2}} \quad \mbox{ and } \quad (1 - i \delta ) A \nabla u_{1, \delta } \cdot \nu = A \nabla u_{ \delta } \cdot \nu \Big |_{+} \mbox{ on } \partial B_{r_{2}}. \tag{3.17}\cssId{TO-1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \left\{\begin{array}{cl} {\mathrm{div}}(A \nabla V_{1, \delta }) + k^2 \Sigma V_{1, \delta } = \displaystyle - \frac {i \delta }{1 - i \delta } k^2 \Sigma u_{1, \delta } \mbox{ in } & B_{r_3} \setminus B_{r_2}, \\[6.0pt] A \nabla V_{1, \delta } \cdot \nu - i k V_{1, \delta } = 0 & \mbox{ on } \partial B_{r_2}, \\[6.0pt] V_{1, \delta } = 0 & \mbox{ on } \partial B_{r_3}. \end{array}\right. \tag{3.18}\cssId{def-V1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| V_{1, \delta }\|_{H^1(B_{r_3} \setminus B_{r_2})} \le C \delta \| u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}. \tag{3.19}\cssId{V1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} U_{1, \delta } =u_{\delta } - u_{1, \delta } - V_{1, \delta }. \tag{3.20}\cssId{def-bU}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} {\mathrm{div}}(A \nabla U_{1, \delta }) + k^2 \Sigma U_{1, \delta } = 0 \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{r_2}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \| U_{1, \delta }\|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r_2})} + \| A \nabla U_{1, \delta } \cdot \nu \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r_2})} \le C \delta \| u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}, \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \| U_{1, \delta }\|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r_3})} + \| A \nabla U_{1, \delta } \cdot \nu \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r_3})} \le C \| u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| U_{1, \delta }\|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{\gamma r_2})} + \| A \nabla U_{1, \delta } \cdot \nu \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{\gamma r_2})} \le C \delta ^{\alpha } \| u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}, \tag{3.21}\cssId{U1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \alpha > 1/2. \tag{3.22}\cssId{alpha-Thm1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \| u_\delta - u_{1, \delta } \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{\gamma r_2})} + \|A \nabla (u_\delta - u_{1, \delta } ) \cdot \nu \|_{H^{-1/2}(\partial B_{\gamma r_2})} \le C \delta ^{\alpha } \| u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}. \tag{3.23}\cssId{part1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} U_{2, \delta } = u_{1, \delta } - u_{2, \delta } + V_{1, \delta }. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \Delta U_{2, \delta } + U_{2, \delta } = 0 \quad \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{\gamma r_2} \tag{3.24}\cssId{eq-U2-Thm1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} U_{2, \delta } = 0 \quad \mbox{and } \quad \partial _r U_{2, \delta } = -\frac {i\delta }{1 - i\delta } \partial _r u_{1, \delta } + \partial _r V_{1, \delta } \quad \mbox{ on } \partial B_{r_3}. \tag{3.25}\cssId{p-eq-U2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \hat{J}_n(t) = 2^n n! J_n(t) \quad \mbox{ and } \quad \hat{Y}_n(t) = - \frac {\pi }{2^{n} (n-1)!} Y_n(t), \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \hat{J}_n (t) = t^{n}\big [1 + o(1) \big ] \tag{3.26}\cssId{bh1}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \hat{Y}_n (t) = t^{-n} \big [1 + o(1) \big ], \tag{3.27}\cssId{bh2}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \begin{split} U_{2, \delta } &= a_0 \hat{J}_0(|x|) + b_0 \hat{Y}_0(|x|)\\ &\quad + \sum _{n=1}^\infty \sum _{\pm } \big [a_{n, \pm } \hat{J}_{n}(|x|) + b_{n, \pm } \hat{Y}_{n}(|x|) \big ] e^{\pm i n \theta } \quad \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{\gamma r_2}, \end{split}\tag{3.28}\cssId{re-u-k}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \partial _r U_{2, \delta } = c_0 + \sum _{n \ge 1} \sum _{\pm } c_{n, \pm } e^{\pm i n \theta } \quad \mbox{ on } \partial B_{r_3}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} |c_0|^2 + \sum _{n \ge 1} \sum _{\pm } n^{-1} |c_{n , \pm }|^2 \sim \|\partial _r U_{2, \delta } \|_{H^{-1/2}(\partial B_{r_3})}^2 \le C \delta ^2 \| u \|_{H^{1}(\Omega )}^2. \tag{3.29}\cssId{pro-c-n}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \left\{\begin{array}{c} a_{n, \pm } \hat{J}_n (r_3) + b_{n, \pm } \hat{Y}_n (r_3) = 0, \\[6.0pt] a_{n, \pm } \hat{J}_n' (r_3) + b_{n, \pm } \hat{Y}_n' (r_3) = c_{n, \pm }, \end{array}\right. \quad \mbox{ for } n \ge 0. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \left\{ \begin{array}{l} \displaystyle a_{n, \pm } = c_{n, \pm } AC_{n}, \\[6.0pt] \displaystyle b_{n, \pm } = c_{n, \pm } BC_{n}, \end{array} \right. \quad \mbox{ for } n \ge 0, \tag{3.30}\cssId{efcd-k}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} AC_{n} = - \frac {\hat{Y}_n}{\hat{J}_n \hat{Y}_n' - \hat{J}_n' \hat{Y}_n}(r_3) \quad \mbox{ and } \quad BC_{n} = - \frac {\hat{J}_n}{\hat{Y}_n \hat{J}_n' - \hat{Y}_n' \hat{J}_n}(r_3). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} AC_{n} = - \frac {1}{2n} r_3^{1-n} \Big ( 1 + o(1) \Big ) \quad \mbox{ and } BC_{n} = \frac {1}{2n} r_3^{1 + n} \Big ( 1 + o(1) \Big ). \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \hat{u}_\delta (x)= \sum _{n=1}^\infty \sum _{\pm } b_{n, \pm } \hat{Y}_{n}(|x|) e^{\pm i n \theta } \quad \mbox{ in } B_{r_3} \setminus B_{\gamma r_2}. \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{equation} \|U_{2, \delta } - \hat{u}_\delta \|_{H^{1/2}(\partial B_{r})} + \|\partial _r U_{2, \delta } - \partial _r \hat{u}_\delta \|_{H^{-1/2}(\partial B_{r})} \le C \delta \|u_\delta \|_{H^1(\Omega )}. \tag{3.31}\cssId{U2-hu}{}{} \end{equation} \]

\[ \begin{equation*} \begin{split} {\mathrm{dim}}\ {\mathrm{C}}_{G}(V,V') & =\frac {1}{2} \left( \sum _{i\geq k, j\geq l}a_{ij}a_{kl}-\sum _{i\geq n+1, j\geq n+1}a_{ij} \right), \quad {\mathit{if}}\ (V,V') \in \mathcal{O}_{\mathfrak{a}},\\ {\mathrm{dim}}\ \mathcal{O}_{\mathfrak{a}} &=\frac {1}{2} \left(\sum _{i<k\ {\mathit{or}}\ j<l}a_{ij}a_{kl}-\sum _{i<n+1 \ {\mathit{or}}\ j<n+1}a_{ij} \right),\\ d(\mathfrak{a})-r(\mathfrak{a}) &=\frac {1}{2} \left(\sum _{i\geq k, j<l}a_{ij}a_{kl}-\sum _{i\geq n+1>j}a_{ij} \right). \end{split} \end{equation*} \]

\[ \begin{align} [\mathfrak{b}] * [\mathfrak{a}] & =\sum _{t: \sum _{u=1}^N t_u=r} v^{\beta (t)}\prod _{u=1}^N \overline {\begin{pmatrix} a_{hu}+t_u\\ t_u \end{pmatrix}}_{\!\!\!{}v}\ [\mathfrak{a}_{t}], \ \mbox{where} \tag{37}\cssId{eq22}{}{}\\ \beta (t) & = \sum _{j\geq l} a_{hj} t_l - \sum _{j>l} a_{h+1, j} t_l + \sum _{j<l} t_j t_l + \frac {1}{2}\delta _{hn}(\sum _{j+l<N+1}t_jt_l+\sum _{j<n+1}t_j), \\ \mathfrak{a}_t & =\left(A+\sum _{u=1}^Nt_u(E^{\theta }_{hu}-E^{\theta }_{h+1,u}),{\mathrm{sgn}}(s_l(\mathfrak{b}), s_r(\mathfrak{a})) \right) \in \Xi _{\mathbf{D}}. \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} [\mathfrak{c}] * [\mathfrak{a}] & =\sum _{t: \sum _{u=1}^N t_u=r}v^{\beta '(t)}\prod _{u=1}^N \overline {\begin{pmatrix} a_{h+1,u}+t_u\\ t_u \end{pmatrix}}_{\!\!\!{}v} \ [\mathfrak{a}(h, t) ], \ \mbox{where}\tag{38}\cssId{eq24}{}{}\\ \beta '(t) & =\sum _{j\leq l} a_{h+1,j} t_l - \sum _{j<l} a_{hj} t_l + \sum _{j<l} t_j t_l, \\ \mathfrak{a}(h, t) &=\left(A-\sum _{u=1}^Nt_u(E^{\theta }_{hu}-E^{\theta }_{h+1,u}), {\mathrm{sgn}}(s_l(\mathfrak{c}), s_r(\mathfrak{a})) \right) \in \Xi _{\mathbf{D}}. \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} [\mathfrak{c}] * [\mathfrak{a}] &= \sum _{t: \sum _{u=1}^N t_u=r}v^{\beta ''(t)} \ \overline {\mathcal{G}}\ [\mathfrak{a}(n,t)], \ \mbox{where}\tag{39}\cssId{eq27}{}{}\\ \beta ''(t)&=\sum _{j\leq l}a_{n+1,j}t_l-\sum _{j<l} a_{nj} t_l\\ &\quad +\sum _{j<l, j+l\geq N+1}t_jt_l + r(r-1)/2-\sum _{j<n+1}t_j (t_j-1) / 2, \\ \mathcal{G} &= \prod _{u<n+1} \begin{pmatrix} a_{n+1,u}+t_u+t_{N+1-u}\\ t_u \end{pmatrix}_{\!\!\!{}v} \cdot \prod _{u> n+1} \begin{pmatrix} a_{n+1,u}+t_u \\ t_u \end{pmatrix}_{\!\!\!{}v} \cdot \prod _{i=0}^{t_{n+1}-1} L_i, \\ L_i & = \frac {(a_{n+1,n+1}+1+2i)_v+(1-\delta _{0,i}\delta _{0, \mathrm{ro}(\mathfrak{a})_{n+1} }) v^{a_{n+1,n+1}+2i}} {(i+1)_v}. \end{align} \]

\[ \begin{align} \sum _{r\leq i, s\geq j} a_{rs} & \leq \sum _{r\leq i, s\geq j} b_{rs}, \quad \forall i<j.\tag{40}\cssId{partial-order}{}{}\\ \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}r\leq n,\\ s>N+1-j \end{subarray}} a_{rs} & \equiv \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}r\leq n,\\ s>N+1-j \end{subarray}} b_{rs} \ \bmod 2, \quad \mbox{if}\tag{41}\\ \mathrm{ro}(\mathfrak{a})_{n+1} & = \mathrm{co}(\mathfrak{a})_{n+1} = 0, \quad \mathrm{ro}(\mathfrak{b})_{n+1} = \mathrm{co}(\mathfrak{b})_{n+1} =0, \\ \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}i\leq r\leq N+1-i,\\ j\leq s\leq N+1-j \end{subarray}} a_{rs} & = \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}i\leq r\leq N+1-i,\\ j\leq s\leq N+1-j \end{subarray}} b_{rs} = 0, \quad \text{and}\\ \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}r<i,\\ s>N+1-j \end{subarray}} a_{rs} &= \sum _{\begin{subarray} {c}r<i,\\ s>N+1-j \end{subarray}} b_{rs}, \quad \forall i, j\in [1,n]. \end{align} \]
